      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☼♄Jülie " class="user" itemprop="url" name="☼♄Jülie " href="/user/show/20814018-j-lie">☼♄Jülie </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25153134-follow-you-home">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20814018-j-lie?shelf=own-kindle-book">own-kindle-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20814018-j-lie?shelf=psychological-thriller">psychological-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20814018-j-lie?shelf=netgalley-for-review">netgalley-for-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1307955963" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4304713803701586156"><br/>Daniel and Laura have had the time of their lives and are now enjoying the last leg of their once in a lifetime European backpacking holiday, before returning home to London to settle down and start a family of their own.<br/><br/>Unable to secure a first class sleeping cabin on the overnight train through Romania, Daniel and Laura settle into their seats to ride out the night. <br/>Laura is uncomfortable with these arrangements and lets Daniel know that she is not impressed with his seemingly cost cutting tra</span>
  <span id="freeText4304713803701586156" style="display:none"><br />Daniel and Laura have had the time of their lives and are now enjoying the last leg of their once in a lifetime European backpacking holiday, before returning home to London to settle down and start a family of their own.<br /><br />Unable to secure a first class sleeping cabin on the overnight train through Romania, Daniel and Laura settle into their seats to ride out the night. <br />Laura is uncomfortable with these arrangements and lets Daniel know that she is not impressed with his seemingly cost cutting travel arrangements, she is tired and can't get comfortable in her seat, and there is a man in the seat across the aisle who keeps staring at her.<br />A young local couple also sitting across the aisle, notice them and change seats to sit opposite them and befriend them, although they seem a little tense at first, they soon get chatting.<br />Sensing Laura's tiredness and discomfort, the couple tell them about an empty sleeping cabin on this carriage that they could use for the next leg of the trip as the guards won't be coming around again for some time. They offer to wake them as that time approaches.<br />Laura is not keen on this idea because she doesn't want to risk getting caught by the guards, but she is so tired that she eventually agrees...after all what's the worst that could happen, they have their passports and tickets and the cabin is empty.<br /><br />Somehow they slept too long and are woken as things go so suddenly and unthinkably wrong when, after some heated and intense altercation with the guards they find themselves thrown off the train at a disused station in the middle of the night, in the middle of nowhere, somewhere in Romania!<br />Along with them is the female half of the couple they befriended on the train!<br /><br />What becomes of them now is so unthinkable that they cannot bear to talk about it...ever!<br />But this journey is just beginning.<br /><br />From the first pages this story has a very high creep factor which quickly picks up pace and maintains a level of creepiness and apprehension that will have you looking behind every door and at every possible angle.<br />I found myself constantly trying to guess at what was going on and not even coming close to finding out until it is eventually revealed.<br /><br />If you like edge of your seat thrillers that keep you guessing, then this is a book for you.<br />With a creep factor of 5 out of 5, this is an intensely gripping read.<br /><br />I gave it 4★s <br /><br />Thanks to NetGalley and the Publishers for my copy to read and review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4304713803701586156" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/25394646-follow-you-home">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1276599275" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12566133138513653183">Mark Edwards is back with a new thriller sure to keep reader up late into the night, especially if they travel by rail. While on a tour of Europe, Laura and Daniel are robbed in the rural townships of Romania, their passports and tickets lifted from their bags. Romanian border guards toss them from the train, along with a young woman, Alina, who sought to defend them. In the middle of nowhere, Alina trudges off and Laura and Daniel soon follow, trying to find her, but only discovering a discarde</span>
  <span id="freeText12566133138513653183" style="display:none">Mark Edwards is back with a new thriller sure to keep reader up late into the night, especially if they travel by rail. While on a tour of Europe, Laura and Daniel are robbed in the rural townships of Romania, their passports and tickets lifted from their bags. Romanian border guards toss them from the train, along with a young woman, Alina, who sought to defend them. In the middle of nowhere, Alina trudges off and Laura and Daniel soon follow, trying to find her, but only discovering a discarded boot. When they come upon a dilapidated house in the forest, Laura and Daniel explore, which is where they plot thickens immensely. Edwards moves the story forward, back to London, where Laura and Daniel sit on a secret they discovered in Romania, one that has left them emotionally and somewhat physically scarred. Neither will talk about it, but they soon drift apart and find themselves on separate tracks as they try to deal with it. Anyone Daniel tells portions of the story to ends up dead, leaving him to wonder if he's being hunted in order to keep quiet. Laura struggles as well, seeing ghosts surrounding her, which pushes her to the brink. Alina's own story adds to the mystery and her appearance in London leaves Daniel to wonder the true and complete story of that house in Romania. Edwards adds layers of thrill and psychological chill in his latest novel, with a cliffhanger or two to blindside the reader as well.<br /><br />Edwards has a knack of building up a happy facade on the periphery of his stories, with a deeper and darker truth to them, the further the book progresses. Once the reader is halfway into the novel, like a masterful web, they cannot escape and must read on to discover what lies behind the next corner. With an interesting background pulled from history, Edwards seeks to thrill the reader into submission. One of his best solo pieces to date, readers will flock to this and devour it more in fear than necessity.<br /><br />Kudos, Mr. Edwards for your sick and twisted ways as you try to keep the reader guessing until the bitter end.<br /><br />Like/hate the review? An ever-growing collection of others appears at: <br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pecheyponderings.wordpress.com/">http://pecheyponderings.wordpress.com/</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12566133138513653183" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oM5WwtQy1vRleEPrepyHoL+fhWtrMPgjnyqHWiJO5x1VZa4PdSObJ/ePRBIt1KGXLSOdkWTfuKIgPZRxLF3QMg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer2558858855299197943">Mark Edwards writes psychological thrillers in which scary things happen to ordinary people.<br/><br/>He loves love hearing from readers and always responds. Mark can be contacted in the following ways:<br/>Email: mark@markedwardsauthor.com<br/>Twitter @mredwards<br/>Facebook: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.facebook.com/markedwardsbooks'>www.facebook.com/markedwardsbooks</a><br/><br/>You can download a free box set of 'Short Sharp Shockers' by visiting <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.markedwardsauthor.com/free'>www.markedwardsauthor.com/free</a><br/><br/>Mark has sold </span>
  <span id="freeText2558858855299197943" style="display:none">Mark Edwards writes psychological thrillers in which scary things happen to ordinary people.<br /><br />He loves love hearing from readers and always responds. Mark can be contacted in the following ways:<br />Email: mark@markedwardsauthor.com<br />Twitter @mredwards<br />Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/markedwardsbooks">www.facebook.com/markedwardsbooks</a><br /><br />You can download a free box set of 'Short Sharp Shockers' by visiting <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.markedwardsauthor.com/free">www.markedwardsauthor.com/free</a><br /><br />Mark has sold over 2 million books since his first solo novel, The Magpies, was published in 2013. Since then he has topped the bestseller lists several times. His other novels are Because She Loves Me, Follow You Home, What You Wish For, The Devil's Work, The Lucky Ones, The Retreat and In Her Shadow. He has also published A Murder of Magpies (a short sequel to The Magpies) and six books co-authored with Louise Voss. <br /><br />Mark lives in the West Midlands, England, with his wife, their three children, two cats and a golden retriever.</span>
